**元智大學 工程學院英語學士班 必選修科目表**

**International Bachelor Program in Engineering at Yuan Ze University**

**List of Required Courses**

**（111學年度入學新生適用）**

**(Applicable to Students Admitted in Academic Year of 2022)**

111.04.20 一一○學年度第六次教務會議通過

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2021, on April 20, 2022

Amended by the 7th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2021, on June 01, 2022

Amended by the 1st Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2022, on September 21, 2022

Amended by the 2nd Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2022, on November 16, 2022

Amended by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2022, on April 19, 2023

For those who would like to registered “Fundamental computer programming”, he/she has to meet the college requirement.. (Course Name: Fundamental Computer Programming)</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="19"><p>外語課程應修習10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，畢業前應修畢三個不同主題式英語課程，共三學期5學分。</li><li>大一英語能力後測「TOEIC模擬測驗」成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」(EL260)。修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」(EL360)計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」。</p><p>凡本校大學部外國學生修習「華語(一)」或「華語(二)」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語(三)」、「華語(四)」。若修習「華語(三)」、「華語(四)」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語(五)」或「華語檢定」(EL372)。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</p><ol><li>English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and Chinese Proficiency Test (EL372).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing(1)、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books(2)、服務學習Service Learning(1)</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education(0)</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education(0)</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education(0)</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education(0)</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="4"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="19"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>(10)★</p></td><td colspan="19"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。</p><p>General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：工程學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課。</p><p>Undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories.</p></td></tr><tr><td University Common Required Course List for General Education course information and regulations.</p><ol><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li></ol><p>The maximum credits for general education courses are 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><ol><li>英語授課課程以「★」表示，包含程式語言4學分、通識教育科目10學分、必修科目35學分及領域必修25-42學分。</li></ol><p>「★」：The credits granted by English-taught courses include 4 credits from Computer Programming, 10 credits from General Education, 35 credits from the department required courses and 25 to 42 credits from the program required courses</p><ol><li>本班必修課程初次修課須在本學程修讀始予承認。</li></ol><p>The compulsory courses have to be taken from the International Program in Engineering for Bachelor for the first time.</p><ol><li>本班同學須自「機械工程」、「化學工程與材料科學」及「工業工程與管理」三個領域中選擇「主修學程」(三選一)或「雙專長學程」(三選二)，並修滿128學分方可畢業。</li></ol><p>Students must choose one major as a「single major」from three fields (i.e., Department of Mechanical Engineering, Department of Chemical Engineering and Materials Science, and Department of Industrial Engineering and Management) or complete two sets of these three fields as a 「double major」.  Minimum credits for graduation: 128 credits.</p><p>「主修學程」領域必修/選修科目請參見附表一。(Annex I-「single major」List of Required and Elective Courses)</p><p>「雙專長學程」領域必修/選修科目請參見附表二。(Annex II-「double major」List of Required and Elective Courses) </p><ol><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li></ol><p>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><p>7.  專業選修除本班各領域共同選修科目表之選修科目外，亦可選修工院各系所、生物科技與工程研究所及其他英語學士班之課程，納入其所需專業選修畢業學分。</p><p>In addition to the elective courses listed in the common elective course table for each major of the program, students </p><p>may also take courses offered by the departments of the College of Engineering, the Graduate School of Biotechnology </p><p>and Bioengineering, and other International bachelor’s programs. These courses may be counted toward the required </p><p>professional elective credits for graduation.</p></td></tr></table>

must choose one major as a「single major」from three fields (i.e., Department of Mechanical Engineering, Department of Chemical Engineering and Materials Science, and Department of Industrial Engineering and Management) or complete two sets of these three fields as a 「double major」.  Minimum credits for graduation: 128 credits.</p><ul><li>「主修學程」領域必修/選修科目請參見附表一。(Annex I-「single major」List of Required and Elective Courses)</li><li>「雙專長學程」領域必修/選修科目請參見附表二。(Annex II-「double major」List of Required and Elective Courses)</li></ul></td></tr></table>

Application (IE212), System Simulation and Applications (IE247), Simulation (IE503), 3D Visual Simulation and Virtual Reality (IE562), Data Visualization (IE574) and Design and Construction of Virtual Reality Systems (IE619) are courses of 'digital application courses'. Reality(IE562), Data Visualization (IE574) and Design and Construction of Virtual Reality Systems (IE619) are courses of 'digital application courses'. Students require passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p></td></tr></table>

courses".</p><ol><li>網路資訊應用課程(IE212)、系統模擬與應用(IE247)、模擬學(IE503)、3D視覺模擬和虛擬實境(IE562)、資料視覺 (IE574)及虛擬實境系統設計與建構 (IE619) 課程為本專長「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本班或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>Network Information Application (IE212), System Simulation and Applications (IE247), Simulation (IE503), 3D Visual Simulation and Virtual Reality (IE562), Data Visualization (IE574) and Design and Construction of Virtual Reality Systems (IE619) are courses of 'digital application courses'. Students require passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p></td></tr></table>

Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and Chinese Proficiency Test (EL372).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing(1)、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books(2)、服務學習Service Learning(1)</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education(0)</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education(0)</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education(0)</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education(0)</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="4"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="19"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>(10)★</p></td><td colspan="19"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。</p><p>General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. major」.  Minimum credits for graduation: 128 credits.</p><p>「主修學程」領域必修/選修科目請參見附表一。(Annex I-「single major」List of Required and Elective Courses)</p><p>「雙專長學程」領域必修/選修科目請參見附表二。(Annex II-「double major」List of Required and Elective Courses) </p><ol><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li></ol><p>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><p>7.  專業選修除本班各領域共同選修科目表之選修科目外，亦可選修工院各系所、生物科技與工程研究所及其他英語學士班之課程，納入其所需專業選修畢業學分。</p><p>In addition to the elective courses listed in the common elective course table for each major of the program, students </p><p>may also take courses offered by the departments of the College of Engineering, the Graduate School of Biotechnology </p><p>and Bioengineering, and other International bachelor’s programs. These courses may be counted toward the required </p><p>professional elective credits for graduation.</p></td></tr></table>

**元智大學 工程學院英語學士班 必選修科目表**

**International Bachelor Program in Engineering at Yuan Ze University**

**List of Required Courses**

**（112學年度入學新生適用）**

**(Applicable to Students Admitted in Academic Year of 2023)**

112.04.19 一一一學年度第六次教務會議通過

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2022, on April 19, 2023

112.05.31 一一一學年度第七次教務會議通過

Amended by the 7th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2022, on May 31, 2023

113.05.01 一一二學年度第八次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 8th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on May 01, 2024

114.04.23 一一三學年度第五次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2024, on April 23, 2025

114.11.12 一一四學年度第三次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 3rd Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2025, on November 12, 2025

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subject</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="5"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="5"><p>第三學年3<sup>rd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="6"><p>第四學年4<sup>th</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>下Spring</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>上Fall</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>下Spring</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>上Fall</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>下Spring</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>上Fall</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>下Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="5"><p>共同必修科目</p><p>Common Compulsory</p><p>（17）</p></td><td><p>國文(一)</p><p>Chinese (I)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>國文(二)</p><p>Chinese (II)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="4"></td><td colspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td><p>英語(一)</p><p>English (I)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>英語(二)</p><p>English (II)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="4"></td><td colspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="19"><p>外語課程應修習10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，畢業前應修畢三個不同主題式英語課程，共三學期5學分。</li><li>大一英語能力後測「TOEIC模擬測驗」成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」(EL260)。修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」(EL360)計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」。</p><p>凡本校大學部外國學生修習「華語(一)」或「華語(二)」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語(三)」、「華語(四)」。若修習「華語(三)」、「華語(四)」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語(五)」或「華語檢定」(EL372)。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</p><ol><li>English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and Chinese Proficiency Test (EL372).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing(1)、經典選讀A Guide to Classics (2)、服務學習Service Learning(1)</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education(0)</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education(0)</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education(0)</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education(0)</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="4"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="19"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>(10)★</p></td><td colspan="19"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。</p><p>General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. （II） for the total 4 credits: English （I） and （II） are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing （EL260） course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” （EL160） is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li><li>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English. The 10 credits in Mandarin Chinese courses must include 2 credits for “Chinese Proficiency Test”. For the specific restrictions and considerations for taking the “Chinese Proficiency Test”, please refer to the 'General Education Foreign Language “English Proficiency Exam” Course Requirements' and 'Yuan Ze University Regulations for Exempting the Mandarin Chinese as a Foreign Language Credit ' for more details.</li><li>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese （I） and （II） before taking Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV）. Students must pass Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV） before taking 'Chinese Proficiency Test' （EL375）.</li></ol><p> 英語檢定English Testing （2）、經典選讀A Guide to Classics （2）、服務學習Service Learning （1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="16"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education（10）</p></td><td colspan="16"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation. </p><p>通識教育科目10學分，須選修英語授課課程。</p><p>These five courses admitted must be the General Education Courses taught in English.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>院必修科目</p><p>College</p><p>Compulsory</p><p>（4）</p></td><td colspan="16"><p>程式語言共4學分，依各院修課規則辦理。(開課名稱：基礎程式設計★)</p><p>Fundamental Computer Programming is a four-credit course. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><ol><li>赴本班所簽訂境外大學修讀雙學位之學生，得申請非本班修讀之必修學分抵免，至多12學分，並於修課前提出。Students pursuing a dual degree program at an overseas university partnered with our program may apply for a maximum of 12 credits of exemption for required courses taken outside our program, and submit an application before enrolling in </li></ol><p>the courses.</p><ol><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</li></ol><p>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p><p>10. 專業選修除本班各領域共同選修科目表(附表三、四)之選修科目外，亦可選修工院各系所、生物科技與工程研究所及其他英</p><p>語學士班之課程，納入其所需專業選修畢業學分。</p><p>In addition to the elective courses listed in the common elective course table(Annex III, IV) for each major of the program, students </p><p>may also take courses offered by the departments of the College of Engineering, the Graduate School of Biotechnology and </p><p>Bioengineering, and other International bachelor’s programs. These courses may be counted toward the required professional elective </p><p>credits for graduation.</p></td></tr></table>

**元智大學 工程學院英語學士班 必選修科目表**

**International Bachelor Program in Engineering at Yuan Ze University**

**List of Required Courses**

**（114學年度入學新生適用）**

**（Applicable to Newly-Admitted Students of 2025）**

114.04.23一一三學年度第五次教務會議通過

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2024, on April 23, 2025

114.11.12 一一四學年度第三次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 3rd Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2025, on November 12, 2025

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subject</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第三學年3<sup>rd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>第四學年4<sup>th</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>上Fall</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>下Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="5"><p>共同必修科目Common Compulsory</p><p>（17）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>中文閱讀、思辨與表達（一）Chinese Reading, Critical Thinking, and Expression （I）</p><p>（2）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>中文閱讀、思辨與表達（二）Chinese Reading, Critical Thinking, and Expression（II）</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>英語（一）</p><p>English （I）</p><p>（2）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>英語（二）</p><p>English （II）</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="11"><ol><li>外語課程應修習 10 學分。</li><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，畢業前應修畢二個不同主題式英語課程，共計 4 學分。</li><li>大一英語能力後測「TOEIC 模擬測驗」成績未達 350 分者，應修習「應試加強班」（EL260）。修習「應試加強班」期間之期末 TOEIC 模擬測驗成績未達 350 分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達 350 分（含）始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」（EL160）計一學期2學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li><li>外國學生可修華語課程10學分，其華語課程 10 學分應含「華語檢定」2 學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」及「元智大學外籍生華語學分抵免規定」。</li><li>凡本校大學部外國學生修習「華語（一）」或「華語（二）」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語（三）」、「華語（四）」。若修習「華語（三）」、「華語（四）」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語檢定」（EL375）。</li></ol><p>1.	The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</p><p>2.	English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</p><p>3.	English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. </p><p>4.	Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </p><p>5.	“English Testing” (EL160) is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</p><p>6.	Foreign students could take 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English. The 10 credits in Mandarin Chinese courses must include 2 credits for “Chinese Proficiency Test”. For the specific restrictions and considerations for taking the “Chinese Proficiency Test”, please refer to the 'General Education Foreign Language “English Proficiency Exam” Course Requirements' and 'Yuan Ze University Regulations for Exempting the Mandarin Chinese as a Foreign Language Credit ' for more details.</p><p>7. The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking 'Chinese Proficiency Test' (EL375).</p><p> 英語檢定English Testing（2）、經典選讀A Guide to Classics（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1） </p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="11"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education（10）</p></td><td colspan="11"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation. </p><p>通識教育科目10學分，須選修英語授課課程。</p><p>These five courses admitted must be the General Education Courses taught in English.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>院必修科目</p><p>College</p><p>Compulsory</p><p>（4）</p></td><td colspan="11"><p>程式語言共4學分，依各院修課規則辦理。</p><p>The Fundamental Computer Programming has 4 credits in total, which General Education, 41 credits from the department required courses and 24 to 38 credits from the program required courses</p><ol><li>本班必修課程初次修課須在本學程修讀始予承認。</li></ol><p>The compulsory courses have to be taken from the International Bachelor Program in Engineering for the first time.</p><ol><li>本班同學須自「機械工程」、「化學工程與材料科學」及「工業工程與管理」三個領域中選擇「主修學程」(三選一)或「雙專長學程」(三選二)，並修滿128學分方可畢業。（自由選修至多承認17學分，含自主學習3學分。）</li></ol><p>Students must choose one major as a「single major」from three fields (i.e., Department of Mechanical Engineering, Department of Chemical Engineering and Materials Science, and Department of Industrial Engineering and Management) or complete two sets of these three fields as a 「double major」.  Minimum credits for graduation: 128 credits. （A maximum of （17） credits can be recognized for free electives, including（3）credits for self-directed learning.）</p><p>「主修學程」領域必修目請參見附表一。(Annex I-「single major」List of Required Courses)</p><p>「雙專長學程」領域必修科目請參見附表二。(<a></a>Annex II-「double major」List of Required Courses)</p><ol><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li></ol><p>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><ol><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計</li></ol><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><ol><li>赴本班所簽訂境外大學修讀雙學位之學生，得申請非本班修讀之必修學分抵免，至多12學分，並於修課前提出。Students pursuing a dual degree program at an overseas university partnered with our program may apply for a maximum of 12 credits of exemption for required courses taken outside our program, and submit an application before enrolling in </li></ol><p>the courses.</p><ol><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</li></ol><p>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p><p>10.  專業選修除本班各領域共同選修科目表(附表三、四)之選修科目外，亦可選修工院各系所、生物科技與工程研究所及其他</p><p>英語學士班之課程，納入其所需專業選修畢業學分。</p><p>In addition to the elective courses listed in the common elective course table(Annex III, IV) for each major of the program, </p><p>students may also take courses offered by the departments of the College of Engineering, the Graduate School of Biotechnology </p><p>and Bioengineering, and other International bachelor’s programs. These courses may be counted toward the required professional </p><p>elective credits for graduation.</p></td></tr></table>
